  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText2910514738122723630" style="display:none"><i>Ryan lowers his lips to my ear. "Dance with me, Beth."<br /><br />"No." I whisper the reply. I hate him and I hate myself for wanting him to touch me again....<br /><br />"I dare you..."</i><br /><br />If anyone knew the truth about Beth Risk's home life, they'd send her mother to jail and seventeen-year-old Beth who knows where. So she protects her mom at all costs. Until the day her uncle swoops in and forces Beth to choose between her mom's freedom and her own happiness. That's how Beth finds herself living with an aunt who doesn't want her and going to a school that doesn't understand her. At all. Except for the one guy who shouldn't get her, but does....<br /><br />Ryan Stone is the town golden boy, a popular baseball star jock-with secrets he can't tell anyone. Not even the friends he shares everything with, including the constant dares to do crazy things. The craziest? Asking out the Skater girl who couldn't be less interested in him.<br /><br />But what begins as a dare becomes an intense attraction neither Ryan nor Beth expected. Suddenly, the boy with the flawless image risks his dreams-and his life-for the girl he loves, and the girl who won't let anyone get too close is daring herself to want it all....</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_421518634" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/421518634" />
    <a title="Marie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6594537-marie"><img alt="Marie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1535710504p2/6594537.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/421518634?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marie" href="/user/show/6594537-marie">Marie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=favourite-series">favourite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer421518634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3957629475834387580"><b> "We lose control- quickly, so fast we've broken beyond floating to flying. I inhale and all I smell is Ryan: the sweet smell of summer rain. I'm so giddy I could almost laugh- I'm finally high. Higher than I've ever been without drugs, higher than I've ever been with other guys, higher than..." </b> <br/><br/>Thoughts <u> <i> BEFORE </i></u>  book:<br/><br/>Wow. What is going on here. It's BETH AND ISAIAH- NOT this Ryan guy whoever the hell HE is. <br/><br/>I'm sorry I'm team Isaiah all the way. I mean c'mon he's such a good guy. He's took c</span>
  <span id="freeText3957629475834387580" style="display:none"><b> "We lose control- quickly, so fast we've broken beyond floating to flying. I inhale and all I smell is Ryan: the sweet smell of summer rain. I'm so giddy I could almost laugh- I'm finally high. Higher than I've ever been without drugs, higher than I've ever been with other guys, higher than..." </b> <br /><br />Thoughts <u> <i> BEFORE </i></u>  book:<br /><br />Wow. What is going on here. It's BETH AND ISAIAH- NOT this Ryan guy whoever the hell HE is. <br /><br />I'm sorry I'm team Isaiah all the way. I mean c'mon he's such a good guy. He's took care of Beth since he's met her. I hope Beth makes the right decision and picks him in the end. <br /><br /><br />Thoughts <u> <i> AFTER </i></u>  book:<br /><br />OK guys I'm very emotionally conflicted about this book. Ill tell you why in a minuet. If I forget about PTL completely and just think of this book as a separate one I could honestly say that Katie McGarry has once again written a fabulous and just as emotional novel full of twists unexpected surprises and secrets. <br /><br />I know this is Beth's book but one of the things I loved most was that Katie still referred back to Echo and Noah when Beth went to see Isaiah. And we got to see how loved up they were and completely happy. I was so glad that we got to see more of them after PTL. <br /><br />As for Beth well she's still the same Beth and she still got me frustrated numerous times especially with all the pesky comments she made about Echo I mean <i> their both damaged goods </i> and hard to understand I thought they would get each other, you know? <br /><br />This book takes you deeper into what happens in Beth's house behind closed doors. And what's behind there <b> isn't pretty </b> let me tell you. <br /><br />After Beth once agains takes the fall for her mothers irrational behaviour, her mothers actions get her locked up. Only for her estranged big shot uncle to take custody of her to keep her mothers dirty secrets silent. <br /><br />Besides everything I think her uncle Scott was very admirable and although he's the first to admit he made a few mistakes. Doesn't everyone? I loved him as a person. His wife Alison wasn't in it much though and i think her character should have been more developed and prominent. I think if she was told and given an explanation for Beth's behaviour she would have been more understanding. <br /><br />Ryan... I hate to say it because it feel like I'm betraying Isaiah. And I've made it no secret that I love Isaiah almost as much as I do Noah.. But Ryan wasn't actually that bad of a guy. In fact he grew on me uncontrollably. Katie has this way with words that make everyone of her characters loved. No matter how much I tried to stay loyal to Isaiah Ryan kept growing on me until I had to admit defeat and acknowledge that I loved him too.<br /><br />One of my favourite parts was when Ryan and Beth finally gave in to their sizzling connection. <br /><br />He may come across all cocky and confident but he has problems just like everyone else. And this is why I'm so conflicted. <br /><br />I guess we all knew in our heart of hearts even though we won't admit it that Beth was going to fall for Ryan. As soon as I saw the description for this book I knew. I tried to cling to a shred of hope. But when I got this book and like PTL was split into Echo and Noah's POV to show their love, DTY was split into Beth and Ryan's. I knew there and then poor Isaiah didn't stand a chance. <br /><br />I kinda feel done over. Like I as made to fall in love with Isaiah in PTL only for me to feel pained by his pain, I wanted to comfort him and tell him he deserved someone better than Beth. We were led to believe that they were undeniably in love with each other in PTL only for it to emerge that Beth in fact thought nothing more about him than her close best friend. I nearly died when Isaiah told her he loved her only for Beth to say I love you too... as my best friend. I could almost feel him shut down. <br /><br />And then when in the beginning he saved her from Trent who makes Beth and her mother his own personal punch bag only for him to say I'm doing it because I love you and she tells him she hates him. Oh GOD Beth could you be even a any more considerate? When your in pain Isaiah is in pain. Don't you get it? <br /><br />Beth doesn't make it easy to like her. Even though in the end I kinda did, it took me a while to forgive her. You'll see when you read the book. In PTL I liked her and gave her the benefit of the doubt because she too was going through a hard time and all she had was Noah and Isaiah and I thought if these two amazing guys liked her then she must be OK.<br /><br />Overall I did very much enjoy this. It didn't shock, or wow me as much as PTL but the quality is still there, McGarry's writing couldn't get better. Its what makes these books so good. <br /><br />I think it would have been easier for me to love this if Isaiah got his happy ending. But I think book 3 might be Isaiah's turn. I just hope McGarry has got him a fantastic lady because if anyone deserves happiness it's him especially since she let Beth get away. <br /><br />I'm not saying that I'm not sad that it didn't turn out the way I wanted it with Beth+Isaiah not becoming a couple but it would have been a little predictable I suppose. And Beth might've still been stuck in the same town as her mother she would never have got her escape. <br /><br />Even so I can't deny this isn't one fabulously written sequel. And you may say you'll hate it because Isaiah and Beth didn't work out but you won't be able to stay true to that after reading this. Like me you'll end up falling for Ryan and just feeling guilty. But if book 3 is Isaiah's book and he gets his HPE we won't have anything to feel guilty about will we? :D that's what I'm hoping for anyway. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3957629475834387580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_460926221" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/460926221" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/460926221?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer460926221" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8995870021640124900"><b>
  <blockquote>There are times when you stand on the cusp of moments so huge, you know you’ll remember them forever. </blockquote>
</b><br/>It all started at a Taco Bell... It was just a dare...<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/f831559f-aa88-415b-baa6-9f04721bee59_zps90669752.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769880.jpg' alt=' photo f831559f-aa88-415b-baa6-9f04721bee59_zps90669752.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> Ryan and his friends never back away from a dare. He and his friend Chris are getting girls numbers... and Chris dares Ryan to get Beth’s. He has no idea what he is in for. She turns him down, but she is still on his mind- <br/><br/>We all remember Noah’s friend Beth from Pushing the Limits...<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/25835f1f-ac0e-4351-bb1c-1bfb2bfda8ec_zps6b25cf58.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769881.jpg' alt=' photo 25835f1f-ac0e-4351-bb1c-1bfb2bfda8ec_zps6b25cf58.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Beth is a bad ass. The tough girl that no one m</span>
  <span id="freeText8995870021640124900" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>There are times when you stand on the cusp of moments so huge, you know you’ll remember them forever. </blockquote>
</b><br>It all started at a Taco Bell... It was just a dare...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/f831559f-aa88-415b-baa6-9f04721bee59_zps90669752.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769880.jpg" alt=" photo f831559f-aa88-415b-baa6-9f04721bee59_zps90669752.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> Ryan and his friends never back away from a dare. He and his friend Chris are getting girls numbers... and Chris dares Ryan to get Beth’s. He has no idea what he is in for. She turns him down, but she is still on his mind- <br><br>We all remember Noah’s friend Beth from Pushing the Limits...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/25835f1f-ac0e-4351-bb1c-1bfb2bfda8ec_zps6b25cf58.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769881.jpg" alt=" photo 25835f1f-ac0e-4351-bb1c-1bfb2bfda8ec_zps6b25cf58.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Beth is a bad ass. The tough girl that no one messes with. Inside, she is not so tough. She has had a hard life. She would do anything for those she loves. That includes protecting her mom. Even though she is sorry drug addict who has never been there for Beth. The only people in her life she can truly count on are her best friends Isaiah and Noah. She and Isaiah have a special relationship. They are best friends, but sometimes they are more than that. If they’ve been drinking. Beth loves Isaiah, but only as a friend. He has other ideas. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Isaiah is my safe. He always has been.</blockquote>
</b> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/f2945220-a3f9-48a9-8c85-70c075d31e79_zps88f46c21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769882.jpg" alt=" photo f2945220-a3f9-48a9-8c85-70c075d31e79_zps88f46c21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Isaiah and Noah want Beth to move in with them, but she can’t. She has to be close to her mom. Then something happens. Beth gets caught in the crosshairs of her mom and loser boyfriends issues, and Beth takes the punishment to save her mom jail time. Her rich Uncle Scott (her dad’s brother turned MLB player) steps in and takes custody of Beth. The last thing she wants to do is move away from her only family, but she has to. It’s the only way to save her mom. <br><br>She gets settled in and is getting read to start school. Beth is unhappy, but she covers it by being a smart ass. While in town, she and her Uncle Scott run into a familiar face. The boy from Taco Bell. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/d920db39-b674-43b6-807e-bb19401dde3b_zps485b73a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769883.jpg" alt=" photo d920db39-b674-43b6-807e-bb19401dde3b_zps485b73a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ryan can’t believe his eyes. As a baseball star looking to play the majors, he runs into one of his idols. Scott Risk. Scott asks a favor of Ryan. Show his niece around, be her friend. Imagine his shock when Scott Risk’s niece happens to be Beth. The girl who lost him the bet. He tries to befriend Beth, but it doesn’t work well. She doesn’t want friends. She wants to figure out a plan to get out of there, save her mom, and run away. With a past relationship, she is leery of Ryan to begin with. She knows his type. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Guys like him don’t go for girls like me. I’m a toy to them. A game. And these types of guys, they all have the same rules of play: smile, trick me into thinking that they like me, then toss me to the side once I’ve been used.</blockquote>
</b><br>I wan’t sure about Ryan to begin with- but like Beth, there is a lot more to him than what is on the outside. Ryan’s life is not as perfect as it seems. His father is constantly pressuring him. Nothing matters except baseball. Nothing. Ryan is a great pitcher, the best. But that is not the only thing he excels at. He is also a fantastic writer. Good enough to final in the state competition. But if it interferes with baseball, his father won’t let him do it. Ryan is caught in at a crossroads in his life. His dad wants him to jump into the majors- but what about what Ryan wants. Would going to college and playing ball be the worst thing?<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/639d3eeb-182a-4c34-bd4c-39bcd8bd9883_zps05dfdbb1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769884.jpg" alt=" photo 639d3eeb-182a-4c34-bd4c-39bcd8bd9883_zps05dfdbb1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Then there is his family drama. His parents aren’t really talking, they won’t let him communicate with his best friend, his brother, who he feels abandoned by. It’s really a mess. His mom is pressuring him to get back with his ex-girlfriend, who is a bitch. It’s just not a good thing. Then- there is Beth. He has never backed away from a challenge, and he’s not about to. The more time he spends with Beth, he realizes there is so much to this girl then he ever imagined. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You’re beautiful when you laugh. You should laugh more.”<br>“Life hasn’t given me much to laugh about.”<br>“I could change that.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>The closer Ryan and Beth become, the more freaked out Beth gets. She and Isaiah aren’t talking much. After he professed his feelings and betrayed her trust, she has no one to really talk to . Ryan wants to be her friend. The bet doesn’t matter anymore. He wants to be there for her, but can she let him?<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Trust me.” “I can’t.” I whisper. I trusted Scott, my mother, and my father. I trusted Luke, my aunt, and Isaiah. All people who left me. All people who faded into darkness. My heart has been ripped multiple times and each time I repaired it on my own. I know my limits and if someone rips me apart again, I’ll never find the strength to pick up the pieces.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/f4cec3c1-162b-4eb5-b446-c3fbe37ad221_zpse60e1dc9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769885.jpg" alt=" photo f4cec3c1-162b-4eb5-b446-c3fbe37ad221_zpse60e1dc9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As their relationship grows and changes, Beth is starting to realize how much Ryan means to her and its scary. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/49ca30ee-c8c3-46a2-8fbf-fdfe58318255_zps16d4d92c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769886._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 49ca30ee-c8c3-46a2-8fbf-fdfe58318255_zps16d4d92c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> Ryan knows how much he cares for Beth. He couldn’t leave her if he wanted. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Leaving her would be like tearing off my own arm. I’ve never been in love before. I thought I had been, but I wasn’t. </blockquote>
</b><br>As I said before, I really wasn't sure about Ryan when I first started this book. With the bet, and my love for Isaiah... I was nervous about how it was going to go. After reading, I have to say that I really love Ryan. He was not perfect, his life was conflicting, he made mistakes, but he really proved himself to me. He was exactly what and who Beth needed in her life. And he needed her just as much. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/4e01a691-3d8a-4d01-8b59-1a48ecf23a79_zpsb140476b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769887.jpg" alt=" photo 4e01a691-3d8a-4d01-8b59-1a48ecf23a79_zpsb140476b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"It's our rain Beth."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Their love grows and it saves them from themselves. I loved the two of them together. Ryan is willing to fight for Beth. To stand up for her, something he has never done in his life. Something big happens in the end- but you will have to read it to find out! <br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“I won't let you go." I blink. As if he could stop me. "You won't let me go." "No, I won't let you go. You're mine and I don't lose.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>This story was AMAZING! Beautiful, heartbreaking and just fabulous! Katie McGarry’s writing is just out of this world. I loved getting both Beth and Ryan’s perspectives. If you loved Pushing the limits, this will be a MUST READ for you! <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/40e66e04-ec6d-4013-bc60-18dd36036ece_zps5af67eca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398396i/769888.jpg" alt=" photo 40e66e04-ec6d-4013-bc60-18dd36036ece_zps5af67eca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>On another note- After reading a preview of Crash Into You (Isaiah’s story) I CANNOT WAIT to read it! He needs a happy ending, and I’m sure it will be just as wonderful as the first two in this series! :D <br><br><i>***ARC provided by Harlequin Limited Publishing via NetGalley in exchange of review***</i></span>

<div id="review_383751164" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/383751164" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/383751164?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      Buddy read with Anna, Ian and Michelle
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer383751164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6320613431318462132"><b>Beth Risk from <i>Dare You To</i> : Otherwise known as a classic example of how to self-sabotage.</b> <br/><br/>3.5 stars. I'll be going against the grain in saying that I liked this book better than the first in the series. I understand that the masses went wild over <i>Pushing the Limits</i>, but I struggled with shakily written stereotypes and repetitive speech patterns. That said, the first book was engaging and the characters were likable, which was enough of a reason for me to want to continue on with the series. <br/><br/>Aft</span>
  <span id="freeText6320613431318462132" style="display:none"><b>Beth Risk from <i>Dare You To</i> : Otherwise known as a classic example of how to self-sabotage.</b> <br /><br />3.5 stars. I'll be going against the grain in saying that I liked this book better than the first in the series. I understand that the masses went wild over <i>Pushing the Limits</i>, but I struggled with shakily written stereotypes and repetitive speech patterns. That said, the first book was engaging and the characters were likable, which was enough of a reason for me to want to continue on with the series. <br /><br />After reading the second book in this series, I'm starting to wonder how much real world experience this author has with kids in non-standard living environments. Maybe she honestly does and I'm just reliving my own personal experiences from a vastly different standpoint. I really don't know. <br /><br />Beth's story is one that I can somewhat relate to. I was kicked out of my original high school (in a rougher, urban area), and my parents felt it would be 'helpful' for me to move away to the sticks in order to gain perspective. I was inwardly cheering that the girl in this story was the troublemaker instead of the boy. I figured this could get interesting.<br /><br />But then...the story started reading like every bad teen movie I'd ever encountered. There was a scene from <i>She's All That</i>, and one from <i>Can't Buy Me Love,</i> and yet another from <i>A Cinderella Story</i>. It was as if I'd fallen into a Molly Ringwald marathon and couldn't get out!<br /><br />One issue that carried over from the first story which I really wish hadn't happened was the demonizing of kids who smoke weed or party in a way not involving the usual and acceptable 'social keg parties.' It made me cringe when Beth was speaking about how it felt to fly as if we were about to be prepared for some public service announcement about the evils of drugs (don't touch, kids! you might want to go throw yourself off a building!). Later in the book, she reflects on how worried she is now that Ryan found out how she used to party. <i>Really? Is this a huge thing to be afraid of? That someone might find out you partied a little too much before you met them?</i> As I stated in my review for book one, if we're going to put certain behaviors in a box as being freaky, we're ostracizing more than the 50% of today's teens who participate in those behaviors. <br /><br />Bad and Good isn't always a black and white thing. Just like being a jock doesn't always equate to being popular, and coming from the wrong side of the tracks doesn't always equate to you getting bad grades or being a screw up. I appreciate what the author is trying to do by exposing the readers to more than a basic 'boy meets girl' story, but I wasn't quite buying the authenticity of it all. <br /><br /><b>YET...this story wasn't so bad.</b> I enjoyed it for the most part. Other than Beth's issues with running and self-doubt, I liked her. She was sassy and didn't let people push her around. I can relate. Ryan was interesting because he was sweet one moment, cocky in another moment, then completely unsure of himself in the next moment. Different waves of behavior such as his somehow felt closer to real the real thing, instead of when you see book guys who are constantly in "worship me" mode. <br /><br />Ryan did have one strange moment of "she is mine" that made me do a double take but it wasn't a deal breaker.<br /><br />So there was a bet. This story started off with a bet. Before you get ready to eye-roll your way on out of here, let me give you this : he told the girl about the bet before the halfway point of the book! HUGE points for this! One big positive about this story is that there wasn't a ton of game playing. Our characters were genuine people who weren't out to deceive others. <br /><br /><b>One other HUGE, MAJOR, MASSIVE plus to this story</b> (mini-spoiler? maybe not) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The guy is the virgin for once! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> *Stacia does imaginary cartwheels all over this review* Woo hoo! Take that, overdone "innocent girl" cliches. <br /><br /><b>You know, the more I think about this book, the more I realize that I really did like it, even with the complaints.</b> The positives do outweigh the negatives - and these positives made the book for me : <br /><br />1. This was a sweet love story.<br />2. The normal gender roles in the relationship were reversed.<br />3. Ryan gave Beth (their) rain in a bottle (won't spoil what this means) because she needed something tangible to hold on to from him other than just pretty words. <br /><br /><i>This book provided from the publisher through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6320613431318462132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_601105366" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/601105366" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/601105366?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer601105366" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18233760088378875404">5 DARE YOU TO STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419228i/830911._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jock v's skater girl ...<br/><br/>This story is written to young adult perfection. The writing is beautifully put together and descriptive. From page one I was hooked. If your looking for a young adult story with depth and emotion then look no further. This author has delivered a novel that i'm sure will capture the attention of most lovers of this genre.<br/><br/>There are so many positives about this book I'm not sure how to write it all coherently in one review, but here are my thoughts ...<br/><br/>As</span>
  <span id="freeText18233760088378875404" style="display:none">5 DARE YOU TO STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419228i/830911._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jock v's skater girl ...<br><br>This story is written to young adult perfection. The writing is beautifully put together and descriptive. From page one I was hooked. If your looking for a young adult story with depth and emotion then look no further. This author has delivered a novel that i'm sure will capture the attention of most lovers of this genre.<br><br>There are so many positives about this book I'm not sure how to write it all coherently in one review, but here are my thoughts ...<br><br>As with most books I read with an Alternative point of view, I felt the bonus of having the opportunity to experience the story from both sides and believe me I loved both Ryan and Beth in equal measure. The story also brilliantly and sensitively tackles the issue of Domestic violence, substance misuse, alcohol dependancy and the dark, sinister reality of a young girl who has suffered at the hands of a troubled upbringing. Expect an explosion of emotions during your reading experience. 'Dare you to' is a heartbreaking, traumatic and captivating story in one gorgeous young adult package. The author has managed to steal my heart and affections, whilst delivering a beautiful message of hope and love.<br><br>So what's the story about, well the authors official blurb sums it up pretty perfectly but from my own words for me this story is all about the gorgeously written characters. <br>Strong, determined, stubborn and fiercely independent Beth Trick has lived her life by the following mantra ~ "if I don't feel, I don't hurt." There is a heavy emptiness about this troubled heroine, Beth has been living a life erecting walls and not allowing anybody in. Following an incident out of her control Beth finds herself taken into the custody of her uncle and his wife. Thrown into a world unknown to Beth she is faced with a new life, new school, new rules, new friends. Leaving behind all that she knows and a life that although was difficult she loved.<br><br>Ryan Stone is a misunderstood rich boy living life by the rules, existing in a world of pretence and order. unknowingly to those around him his family and all that he knows to be secure is falling apart. From the outside it looks like he has it all ~ wealth, popularity and the high school baseball star. Ryan is an extremely loveable character, he is the epitome of gorgeous hero, with a golden heart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419228i/830912._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419228i/830913._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, What happens when love crosses boundaries. When everything that Ryan and Beth thought made sense changes, shifts and become a kaleidoscope reality. What happens when love changes everything? <br><br>This novel is a story of two lost hearts finding each other, and at the same time saving themselves, but it's much more than a chance love encounter... Don't miss out on this story of Beth and Ryan and what happens when love doesn't make sense and dares to become reality.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419228i/830914._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a gorgeously written story that I loved from beginning to end. For those who are fans of book one in the series we also get a glimpse into the lives of past characters. I for one can't wait to read more, and I'm excited about what the author is going to deliver next.<br><br>Favourite quotes from the book ~<br><br>❤❤“That must be love: when everything else in the world could implode and you wouldn't care as long as you had that one person standing beside you.” <br><br>❤❤“I won't let you go." I blink. As if he could stop me. "You won't let me go." "No, I won't let you go. You're mine and I don't lose.” <br><br>❤❤“Guys like you don't fall for girls like me.” <br><br><br>5 HUGE 'CAN' STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419228i/830915._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*ARC Generously provided by Harlequin UK via Netgalley*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="18233760088378875404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_410590548" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/410590548" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/410590548?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=to-ya-or-not-to-ya">to-ya-or-not-to-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer410590548" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13559943260857174009">Pushing the Limits, excuse my profanity, is a bastard to follow up on. It was such an emotional, powerful book, so neat and well-constructed, that I was wary to pick up the next one. I needn’t have been entirely terrified, Dare You To is still a pretty good book with enjoyable things to reccomend it. I simply didn’t love it as much as I wanted to. I didn’t even cry once. It made me question, for a moment, if McGarry had lost her touch to regularly make me bawl like a little baby who got pricked </span>
  <span id="freeText13559943260857174009" style="display:none">Pushing the Limits, excuse my profanity, is a bastard to follow up on. It was such an emotional, powerful book, so neat and well-constructed, that I was wary to pick up the next one. I needn’t have been entirely terrified, Dare You To is still a pretty good book with enjoyable things to reccomend it. I simply didn’t love it as much as I wanted to. I didn’t even cry once. It made me question, for a moment, if McGarry had lost her touch to regularly make me bawl like a little baby who got pricked by their first vaccination.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390620ra/752429.gif" alt="crying man" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A big, angry, devastated baby<br><br>To me, it’s construction and execution didn’t seem as tight and effortlessly fluid as Pushing the Limits. In Pushing The Limits, it really felt like the the characters and their relationships with each other, with the world, with their flawed perceptions were all part of an intricate dance in a wonderful universe where everything made sense. WHY DOESN’T EVERYTHING MAKE SENSE, MCGARRY?! WHY?! MAKE IT BETTER FOR ME!<br><br>In Dare You To, Beth, Noah’s goth friend from Pushing the Limits, is separated from her drug-addicted mother and forced to live with her rich uncle. This means:<br><br>New school<br><br>New town<br><br>New friends<br><br>No drugs, drinking or random hook ups.<br><br>This would be a lot of difficult life changes on their own but then comes Ryan. Perfect awesome school dude who has his own set of problems.<br><br>Only Ryan’s life isn’t perfect. His brother’s been kicked out of home and his parents hate each other. The unlikely couple is forced together and form a relationship that is sweet and respectful and nothing that Beth has ever had before.<br><br>So first issue: Dude, what happened with Isaiah? And no disrespect because this author is badass and everything. I just happened to kind of be shipping toward Isaiah/Beth because things just seemed to be driving at break neck speed in that direction. The direction in which my heart sings, double rainbows break out and I get to go live in Equestria with all my pony friends (Rainbow Dash, we would be the best of friends).<br><br>But, you know, I liked Ryan in the end. He was cool. Real cool. Romantic too. There were some nice gestures there, bro.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390620ra/752430.gif" alt="Cool job, bro. Thumbs up." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In fact, he was so nice, the only real relationship I ended up contesting was Beth and her uncle’s. Ultimately, I could imagine Beth deciding she didn’t love Isaiah. That’s cool. Ultimately I could reconcile Beth’s 180 change in characterization, despite my issues with its story line. But the one thing I struggled with was the relationship between Beth and Scott, because this was a really pivotal relationship for Beth’s character development, and I was totally not feeling it. A good portion of the initial respect and tolerance between them is developed off page.<br><br>And then it just kind of takes a jagged, cutesy path that I didn’t feel was a natural progression. Of course, it doesn’t help that Beth had to change a lot in ways that I felt were unnecessary. Like you can’t be a good character if you dress like a goth, smoke some weed and like to drink occasionally. I guess I just felt it was hard to watch Beth change to other people’s expectations when a lot of those were a result of needs that didn’t seem to be met.<br><br>“I need to be there for my mother! I’ll give everything to help her- no wait. I’m cool. Totes seen the error of my ways. Let’s party, aye, Ryan?”<br><br>However, no matter how you feel, it’s still a well written, nice contemporary romance that made me all squishy inside. Up to individual tastes, but most people will mostly like it, so go ahead!<br><br>I’m not entirely sure if this review made sense because alcohol, drugs, and dressing in black seem to be a bad combination according to this book. But I guess, what I wanted, was more acceptance of Beth’s actual issues, as opposed to the outward issues. And that never seemed to be addressed fully. Her pain, her issues, were kind of swept aside with platitudes.<br><br>And, frankly, I was just in the mood for hardcore truths and badass emotional situations. Having a nice, lovely novel was good, but it just wasn’t the awesomeness I expected from McGarry. Because I love her. And I kind of wanted Unicorns and double rainbows, and Rainbow Dash to read me my favourite book.<br><br>Wait… I can still get that, right?<br><br><i>This ARC was provided to me by Harlequin. No money, gifts or favors were exchanged for this review. I mean, I tried to get some but they wouldn't answer my calls and then they were always busy...<br></i><br><b>This review, and more like it, can also be found on my blog, <a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/blog/2013/05/25/review-dare-you-to-by-katie-mcgarry/" rel="nofollow noopener">Cuddlebuggery Book Blog</a>.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13559943260857174009" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_466306722" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/466306722" />
    <a title="nick (the infinite limits of love)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love"><img alt="nick (the infinite limits of love)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606193187p2/2993271.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466306722?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="nick (the infinite limits of love)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="nick (the infinite limits of love)" href="/user/show/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love">nick (the infinite limits of love)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466306722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4332110005959775496">Katie McGarry wowed me with her debut, Pushing the Limits, last year. I was a little bit hesitant to start Dare You To because it was Beth's story and I never really liked her character in the book. Plus, she wasn't going to be with Isaiah, who clearly really loved her. But then, the cover came out! And well, you probably just guessed what happened!<br/><br/>Like I mentioned above, Beth was never really a character that I enjoyed. When I started Dare You To, I decided to temporarily forget my feelings for</span>
  <span id="freeText4332110005959775496" style="display:none">Katie McGarry wowed me with her debut, Pushing the Limits, last year. I was a little bit hesitant to start Dare You To because it was Beth's story and I never really liked her character in the book. Plus, she wasn't going to be with Isaiah, who clearly really loved her. But then, the cover came out! And well, you probably just guessed what happened!<br><br>Like I mentioned above, Beth was never really a character that I enjoyed. When I started Dare You To, I decided to temporarily forget my feelings for her. However, that didn't really help me. My annoyance with her character amplified by ten-fold. She was a really frustrating character. I guess I should have expected it, but her constant bitchy attitude nearly ruined this book for me. She was angry and rude all the time, making it very hard to grow fond of her. I thought I should give it some time, to let her grow, but her growth took forever. Now, she had a lot going on in her life and I understood her circumstances, but did she really have to spew venom at every person who tried to help her out? Beth's life was anything but easy. She lived with her drug addict mother who had a violent and abusive boyfriend. Beth's mother was a sorry excuse for a mother. It was horrible that Beth was the one who had to look after her when it should have been the other way round. It was painful to watch Beth try to do everything she could to help her mother out when all her mother did was continue to justify the abusive bastard who hit her daughter. I must say that although I thought it was outrageous that Beth continued to help her mom out, at the same time, I appreciated her bravery and devotion to her. With everything that had occurred in her life, Beth was bitter towards everyone and had huge trust issues, so she failed to see the love that her uncle Scott has for her when he adopts her. Towards the end of the book though, she managed to grow a little, appreciating the fact that she had people who loved and supported her and learning to do the right thing. Still, it was very hard for me to connect with her character.<br><br>Ryan, the other main character, seemed to be the jock with the perfect life from the exterior, but that was just the exterior. His home life was really messed up with his parents bossing him around and manipulating his every action. Plus, his brother who had come out had left because his parents wouldn't accept the fact that he was gay. So, Ryan felt abandoned by the person that he loved the most. Initially, Beth was only a dare to Ryan. But over the course of the book, he gets really know her and slowly starts to fall for her. Their relationship was full of ups and downs, downs especially because Beth was reluctant to let anyone get close to her. Fortunately, Ryan wasn't one to give up so easily and continues to push Beth into places she was scared to go to. His adamant nature went well with Beth's fiery one. I thought they complemented each other very well. Initially, when the two of them were together in a scene, all I could see was hostility, but this hostility evolved into sparks slowly. Although both of them were physically attracted to each other from the very beginning, it did take some time for their relationship to grow and I really appreciated the slowness of the romance. Like Pushing the Limits, this book was told in dual POVs and I thought Katie McGarry handled it splendidly once again. She's very good at writing multiple POVs and I hope she continues to do so in her subsequent books. McGarry is also very good at writing realistic books with so many serious and intense themes. I have to admit though that I'm slightly disappointed with her for not having more of Isaiah in this book, but I'm going to forgive her for that because the next book is going to be all about him! My heart broke into pieces for him in this book, so I can't wait to see him find his HEA.<br><br>Fans of Pushing the Limits will definitely appreciate Dare You To because it was as good as the former. although it might take some time to get accustomed to Beth's voice. Once again, Katie McGarry has nailed it with her intense contemporary novel and I'm definitely looking forward to reading more from this talented woman.<br><br>&lt;3_&lt;3<br>That cover ...<br><br><a href="http://s63.beta.photobucket.com/user/Shanika_06/media/tumblr_lxk89ajihM1r8j6pgo1_400.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399185ra/772177.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My first reaction on seeing the cover<br><br><a href="http://s63.beta.photobucket.com/user/Shanika_06/media/tumblr_m8shrwxto01ruz64f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391560ra/754047.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then I went like this<br><br><a href="http://s63.beta.photobucket.com/user/Shanika_06/media/I_like_to_move_it.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399185ra/772178.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But then I saw the release date<br><br><a href="http://s63.beta.photobucket.com/user/Shanika_06/media/Santana_Crying.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399185ra/772179.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh well! Until then, I'll just be like this <br><br><a href="http://s63.beta.photobucket.com/user/Shanika_06/media/tumblr_lgkbl195BA1qfmbjao1_400.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399185ra/772180.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer8257328734340973463"><br/><b> CAN or CAN'T? This is the question... </b><br/><br/>I finished this one a few days ago so my review might not make sense. Just a few thoughts, okay?<br/><br/>I love YA! Yeah, I know, I keep selling myself like an erotica reader but what really grabs me is a good YA story and this one was pretty good.<br/><br/>I love hate/love relationships. They are the best for me and let's say Beth was not a big fan of Ryan when they met at Taco Bell. <br/><br/><b><blockquote>"There is absolutely nothing you can do to ever get me to give you my name or number"<br/>"I bet </blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8257328734340973463" style="display:none"><br><b> CAN or CAN'T? This is the question... </b><br><br>I finished this one a few days ago so my review might not make sense. Just a few thoughts, okay?<br><br>I love YA! Yeah, I know, I keep selling myself like an erotica reader but what really grabs me is a good YA story and this one was pretty good.<br><br>I love hate/love relationships. They are the best for me and let's say Beth was not a big fan of Ryan when they met at Taco Bell. <br><br><b><blockquote>"There is absolutely nothing you can do to ever get me to give you my name or number"<br>"I bet I can"<br>"Can't" </blockquote> </b><br><br>There are people than can't dream. Well, they can but they also know their dreams won't come true and this was Beth's situation. She had a shitty life, a shitty family and a shitty future... So can she or can't she change that and dare to dream of a new life?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428755i/858175.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>People like Beth build walls and never let them down but what happens when someone is attempting to let your walls down over and over and over again?<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>People who make me feel are worse. If I don't feel, I don't hurt </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428755ra/858176.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryan is one of those guys who apparently has a perfect life. But, what is perfect? Have you ever think about the meaning of perfection??? Being perfect means doing what YOU think is perfect or doing what OTHERS think is perfect for your life?<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> How many of us will have the courage to be ourselves regardless of what others think? </blockquote>
</b><br><br>What will happen when perfect Ryan and imperfect Beth collide? Go read this book and find out.</span>

<div id="review_354454959" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/354454959" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/354454959?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer354454959" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4434040126042815874">Well, Katie McGarry just wowed me again! <b>Dare to You</b> was just as <b>
  <i>AMAZING </i>
</b>if not more that Pushing the Limits!! I was full of intense emotions, and on the edge of my seat the entire read, completely immersed in Beth and Ryan’s story!! <br/><br/>I knew Beth’s story would be something else, because she was such a hard and troubled character in Pushing the Limits, and now we finally see why. Beth is living with her aunt after having the crap beat out of her by her mother’s boyfriend, Trent (what a gem!). </span>
  <span id="freeText4434040126042815874" style="display:none">Well, Katie McGarry just wowed me again! <b>Dare to You</b> was just as <b>
  <i>AMAZING </i>
</b>if not more that Pushing the Limits!! I was full of intense emotions, and on the edge of my seat the entire read, completely immersed in Beth and Ryan’s story!! <br /><br />I knew Beth’s story would be something else, because she was such a hard and troubled character in Pushing the Limits, and now we finally see why. Beth is living with her aunt after having the crap beat out of her by her mother’s boyfriend, Trent (what a gem!). Her mother is a loser and that’s putting it mildly, but Beth still feels obligated to make sure she’s okay. When an altercation ends in Beth taking the fall for her mother with the law, Beth ends up in her Uncle Scott’s custody. Beth hasn’t seen Scott in years since he left Beth and she does not welcome his return. She has nothing but resentment and anger at him for abandoning her to the hell her life has become. <br /><br />Ryan’s life is perfect. At least, that’s what it looks like from the outside. He’s the all-American boy with everything going for him: good looks, promising future in baseball, and a well respected family. What they don’t know is Ryan’s family is falling apart behind the scenes. His parents look like the model couple outside but can barely stand each other behind closed doors. His older brother Mark has been ousted from the family, and Ryan resents and mourns his absence. Ryan had his own struggles, trying to figure out his future. For so long he goes along with his parent’s expectations and desires, but is this what will make him happy?<br /><br />When a dare brings Beth and Ryan together their worlds collide. They are from very different backgrounds but there’s a spark of attraction between them. At first you can’t tell if they want to kiss or kill each other! But shared troubles bring them together and they start to form a bond. Romance lovers will not be disappointed, because there is plenty of swoon is this novel!! <br /><b>
  <i><br />“We should talk,” I say in a rush before the thought drifts away, but my hand draws another lazy circle on her stomach. Her muscles come alive under my touch, a shudder of pleasure, and I crave to please her. <br />“No, we shouldn’t,” she answers. “Talking is overated.”*</i>
</b><br /><br />I had a stupid happy grin at just about everything Ryan did!! In a sea of “bad-boy” characters, Ryan stands out as a good-guy who melts your insides!! <br /><b>
  <i><br />I want her to be wowed so she’ll stay on homecoming court, but more…I want this gift to prove that I know her and that I see beyond black hair and nose rings and cut-up jeans. I see her as she really is—I see Beth.* </i>
</b><br /><br />*sigh*<br /><br />Beth was so guarded and hesitant to trust, but you really couldn’t blame her for feeling that way. How can you trust outsiders when your family has let you down so many times and in infinite ways? My heart soared when she finally started letting people in. <br /><br />Ryan has led such a sheltered life, but his family raised him right,<i> for the most part.</i> How else could you have such a complete gentleman? I can’t express how much I loved and respected his behavior!! The way he treated Beth is what finally made her walls come down and begin to trust. Scott was also a huge part of Beth’s road to healing, and it was nice to finally see a responsible, present and loving adult in YA fiction!! <br />	<br />Ms. McGarry is fast becoming a favorite author of mine, she has a talent for writing amazing and well-fleshed out characters that make you care. Such a moving, emotional, and riveting story! <b>Dare to You</b> is one of my favorite reads of 2013!!<br /><br /><i>A copy was provided by Harlequin Teen through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /><br />*Quotes taken from an uncorrected proof and may change in the final copy.<br /><br />You can read this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/04/review-dare-to-you-by-katie-mcgarry.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4434040126042815874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer607930742" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6872362369642375742"><b>
  <u> I received this ARC in exchange for an honest review </u>
</b><br/><br/><b>This book was very clearly NOT FOR ME. It was so NOT FOR ME that I refuse to even finish or review it. Here are my reading notes: </b><br/><br/>Two perspectives, guy and girl, love that. <br/><br/>Ew. Chris, Mr. MC's bestie? Has an “awesome” girlfriend yet is playing the “lemme get your number” game? Total skeeze move.<br/> <br/><i>"All girls are the same...All girls want the same thing. A guy who shows interest."</i> Really, Mr. MC who I’m supposed to like? Really? <br/><br/>Hmmm, Beth’s</span>
  <span id="freeText6872362369642375742" style="display:none"><b>
  <u> I received this ARC in exchange for an honest review </u>
</b><br><br><b>This book was very clearly NOT FOR ME. It was so NOT FOR ME that I refuse to even finish or review it. Here are my reading notes: </b><br><br>Two perspectives, guy and girl, love that. <br><br>Ew. Chris, Mr. MC's bestie? Has an “awesome” girlfriend yet is playing the “lemme get your number” game? Total skeeze move.<br> <br><i>"All girls are the same...All girls want the same thing. A guy who shows interest."</i> Really, Mr. MC who I’m supposed to like? Really? <br><br>Hmmm, Beth’s basically a bitch to Mr. MC immediately, can't say I blame her at this point. When he tries to talk to her she asks him if he’s as stupid as he looks…<br><br>Um…girls shouldn’t swear? Really??? Hey, Mr. MC who I’m supposed to like, <b>FUCK YOU. </b><br><br><u>*Switch to Beth's perspective*</u><br><br>“skater chick” who as far as I can tell doesn’t skate. <br><br>Opening scene w her and she’s high. <br><br><i>“We only touch when we’re high or drunk or both…”</i> (talking about her and Isaiah) That sounds healthy. Can’t wait to read more about how fucked up you are…<br><br>Mother’s a rowdy alcoholic that thrives on sick men. Yuck?<br><br>She can’t move in with Isaiah and Noah because she needs to live two blocks from her mom to clean up her shit? Eff that nutjob, live your own life. <br><br>Pg 27. Wow. Just wow. I repeat, fuck. That. Nutjob. <br><br>Why do people let relatives treat them like trash? Just because they share some genetics? <br><br>Jesus. This is fucked up. Beth's mom is basically the worst person ever. She's convinced Beth that everything that’s wrong with her life is Beth’s fault. Fuck you lady. You hear me? Your daughter won't say it so I will: <b> FUCK. YOU. </b><br><br>Beth's mom busts out the windows of her boyfriend’s car because he cheated. You know, the one that beat up her and her daughter and she’s still with? He catches her and hits her. Shocking. Beth picks up the baseball bat to defend her mom and that’s when the cops show up. <br><br>The boyfriend blames Beth for knocking out the windows of the car. Mom’s on probation and silently pleads that she takes the blame SO BETH FUCKING DOES. <br><br>What…what is this shit? Why do so many people like this? DRAMA DRAMA DRAMA DRAMA. How much drama can you fit in one book? And how much STOOPID???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/464106.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>*Snap to Ryan*</u><br><br>Mr. MC who I’m supposed to like is pitching in a baseball game. <br><br>Is this one of those books where every time I get super pissed the perspective changes and I get dragged back in? I hope not. <br><br>Ryan's parents are together. Mom wears pearls and prays in public. Obvious total opposite of Beth’s mom. Sigh. Really? SUPER STEREOTYPES IN THE WHOLE BOOK? <br><br>His ex, Gwen, is there with her long blonde hair, long legs and her new guy. Chris (Mr MC’s best bro) tells her she’s into him again. Ugh. <br><br>Chris’s girlfriend Lacy doesn’t seem that bad. Calls Gwen evil. Ryan is too stupid to see past her sparkly exterior to the ugly beneath. <br><br>I don’t know if I can read this shit. <br><br><u>*Back to Beth*</u><br><br>In jail. In full blown Nicotine withdrawal. <br> <br>Keeps her mouth shut to protect her mom, subsequently protecting her mom's super-douche of a boyfriend. <br><br>Beth wonders how the cops know she doesn’t live with her mom. YOU’RE IN FOSTER CARE. THERE ARE RECORDS, DUMBASS. <br><br>Thinks she’d rather GO TO JAIL then send her mom there because <i>“Mom can’t hack jail”</i>??? No, mom NEEDS to go to jail you FIDIOT. ARGH!<br><br>Uncle on father’s side to the rescue. Got the charges against her dropped. Wants her to come live with him. Decent guy?<br><br>OH. MY. GOD. No. No he's not. He blackmails her mom into turning her over into his care. “Give me the kid and I won’t tell the cops the shit I saw in your house.”<br><br>Fuck it. I can’t fucking do this. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414796i/818110._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://litchickhitlist.blogspot.com/2013/05/dare-you-to-by-katie-mcgarry.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380236610i/681458._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

<div id="review_1524667184" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1524667184" />
    <a title="may ❀" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49148508-may"><img alt="may ❀" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562443036p2/49148508.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1524667184?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="may ❀" class="user" itemprop="url" name="may ❀" href="/user/show/49148508-may">may ❀</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49148508-may?shelf=400-pgs">400-pgs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49148508-may?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49148508-may?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1524667184" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13057885452310489139"><br/>This book was way longer than I initially anticipated it to be. I’ve had mixed feelings throughout reading it, but in the end, I was glad that I stuck with it. <br/><br/><i> Dare You To </i> is the sequel to <i> Pushing The Limits </i> and follows the story of Beth (who we previously met) and Ryan. Beth’s home life is a private and troubling matter that she is not willing to share with anyone. In attempts to protect her mother from going to jail, Beth finds herself in an unfortunate predicament that leaves her with no </span>
  <span id="freeText13057885452310489139" style="display:none"><br />This book was way longer than I initially anticipated it to be. I’ve had mixed feelings throughout reading it, but in the end, I was glad that I stuck with it. <br /><br /><i> Dare You To </i> is the sequel to <i> Pushing The Limits </i> and follows the story of Beth (who we previously met) and Ryan. Beth’s home life is a private and troubling matter that she is not willing to share with anyone. In attempts to protect her mother from going to jail, Beth finds herself in an unfortunate predicament that leaves her with no other option than to move in with her uncle. Beth now has to combat a new aunt, a new school, and new classmates, specifically golden-baseball-star, Ryan Stone. These two characters have their worlds collide and they are forced to deal with each other, all the while trying to find who they really are underneath their concrete facades. <br /><br />In comparison to the first book, I found this book to be a little forced (and frustrating). It should be well known that I am not one to typically fangirl over sequels (hush, I’ll make as many exceptions as I please) so that might be contributing to my initial hesitancy towards this book. <br /><br />The characters took some time to accept whereas I felt an immediate likeness towards Echo (and Noah) in Pushing the Limits. Maybe that partially because we’ve had a previous glimpse at Beth’s character, but for some reason I found it hard to latch onto the story and lose myself in it. <br /><br />I did eventually become engrossed in the story and found myself cheering the two dorks on and gushing like a little girl (though it was accompanied by many eye rolls and exasperated sighs - yes, Ryan is <i> slightly </i> too cheesy). This book was enjoyable to read, don’t get me wrong, but I felt that it was too drawn out. <br /><br />I was super happy that we got little cameos of Noah and Echo *squeals* albeit they could have been longer and more frequent, but I was happy to see the little babies again (even if they were being gross). <br /><br />I have to say, I quite enjoyed the character development in this book. Seeing Beth mature, open up, and build a wonderful bond with her uncle was very touching. <br /><br />I’m pretty sure I am not yet done with this series. So stay tuned. <br /><br /><i> There are times when you stand on the cusp of moments so huge, you know you’ll remember them forever. </i><br /><br />3.5 stars!!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13057885452310489139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I'm using plural because they were two different stories who connected and became one... And that i love too much in these books. That we have a dual POV! So we understand the things better and from every part....<br/>Oh, my Gosh!!! I really don't know how to start...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381455275ra/4889688.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>In Echo and Noah's story, we met Isaiah and Beth... For Isaiah, i will talk to you in t</span>
  <span id="freeText17534763580386632477" style="display:none">Whoa!!!! The second book was also... Whoa!!!.... Amazing!!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397103ra/765976.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I really liked these series very much, and i liked even more Beth and Ryan's stories... I'm using plural because they were two different stories who connected and became one... And that i love too much in these books. That we have a dual POV! So we understand the things better and from every part....<br>Oh, my Gosh!!! I really don't know how to start...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381455275ra/4889688.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>In Echo and Noah's story, we met Isaiah and Beth... For Isaiah, i will talk to you in the next book.... But Beth, i swear to you that I didn't like that girl at all... I knew that her life sucked but she was mean to Echo because of the change that she brought to Noah.... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424267733ra/13736221.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She was a major bitch and in the beginning of her book, she wasn't much different than the previous... Her language was bad, her attitude was bad.... Okay she was a bad-ass girl and a fighter and she didn't take bullshits from noone... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427991107ra/14347830.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>But then i was starting to see some glimpses of her soul... <br>And there were hidden treasures of a lost girl who used to love ribbons.... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420509i/834141.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But there was also fear and loyalty and low self-respect... <br>She had a really dificult life... All her life she was trying to take care of her mother who was alcoholic and drug addict and she was having a boyfriend that loved to hit her and especially he was enjoying to hit Beth a lot!!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427991107i/14347831._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Her only shelter was Noah and Isaiah... Her best friends, but with Isaiah was more close... He was her anchor... Until everything changed....<br><br>Ryan was a beautiful and nice guy!!! Everybody loved him!!!! He was living the perfect life.... He was the best pitcher in baseball team, he was living in a perfect house with his perfect parents... All his life was organised and planned in advanced!!! <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410810i/806008._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But behide closed doors, you never know what really happens.... His perfect life wasn't so perfect after all, but he was trying to remain strong and to keep up with the plan... His only enjoyment was the dares that made with his friends... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427991107i/14347833.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The dares was giving him such a rush!!! After all he was born a winner and he didn't accept anything else than the win... <br><br>In a dare Beth and Ryan's paths collide with the result not in Ryan's favor. He lost a dare for first time.... But when everything changed in Beth's life and she had to move in with her uncle, Ryan was having one more chance of winning.... <br>But the hearts have their own minds and when they start to beat very fast, you have to hear them....<br><br>I liked Beth's spirit... <br>She was wild, untamed, fiercy at the outside... But inside was a scared little girl... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429622i/860790.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>A girl who was afraid of love and became willingly numb... <br>But when she starts to feel, she's trying all the time to run away....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427991107ra/14347835.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>And i liked Ryan... He was strong and steady.... And when he loves, he is doing it with all his heart.... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420509i/834140._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Love liberated him in every possible way and i liked the fact that i became a witness in his liberation....<br><br>I also have to refer to Isaiah, Noah and Echo, who i loved from the first moment.... Also i liked too much Scott and Lacy, Logan and Chris... And of course, Mark... They were good guys!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427991107ra/14347836.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I want to say that i didn't like Gwen, she was the real bitch!!!! And also i despise Ryan's father... He was a manipulating pig.... <br>As for Beth's mother??? I don't know... I feel angry with her, but also i feel pity for her... Obviously, she lost her way in some point, but she loved her daughter... But i couldn't ever forgive her if i was Beth!!!! Her actions was unforgivable....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427991107ra/14347837.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17534763580386632477" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
